name:Y‚Äça‚Äço‚Äçm‚Äçi‚Äçn‚Äçg‚Äçd‚Äçi‚Äçd‚Äçi
info:2 Twin Beds Standard
info:Stayed in July 2023

posted:Posted July 19, 2023
msg:[Shentie Crowne Plaza] Can be one, more can be repeated

[Purpose] Three days and two nights, self-driving in summer, family travel, elderly

[Check-in] Two nights in a double bed (including breakfast) + double bed room, of which the double bed room will be upgraded to an "L-shaped" superior viewing double bed room after arriving at the store, overlooking the southwest and northwest directions.

[Experience] Staying at Shenzhen Railway Crowne Plaza for the third time, each time has a different feeling.

For the first time, I led a team to Shenzhen University for exchange 2 years ago. The hotel next to the university has a convenient location. It was the first time I boarded the lobby on the 46th floor. Through the full floor-to-ceiling glass, I looked around the Nanshan Mountains in Shenzhen in the four directions of the southeast, northwest, and the Lau Fau Mountain in Yuen Long on the other side of the Shenzhen Bay. It was very shocking. The rooms are not particularly large, but comfortable and elegant. Each room has a transparent floor-to-ceiling window overlooking the buildings along Shennan Avenue, giving you the feeling of "king of the world". But because I had a mission at the time, I spent most of my time outside and rarely stayed in the hotel, so I didn't have a deep sense of experience.

The second time, also in the late autumn 2 years ago, I traveled by car with my wife and arranged to stay in Shenzhen for one night as the last stop before returning to Guangzhou. I booked InterContinental Dameisha, but was let go, so I decided to go back to Crowne Plaza Shenzhen Railway. It was already 10 o'clock in the evening when I arrived at the store, and the front desk paid for check-in. I didn't have much experience in a hurry, and the main thing was peace of mind. However, there was a small episode, that is, after leaving the store, I found that I booked the same room through Ctrip, and breakfast was included at the same price. I called the hotel on the way back, and got a reply that "the next time I enter the store, I will get two additional breakfasts", which also left a foreshadowing for the third stay.

The third time, I stayed again a few days ago, focusing on peace of mind and familiarity. Traveling with my 70-year-old parents, I didn't dare to try too many new things, so I booked back to Shenzhen Railway Crowne Plaza. There are several aspects to consider:

1. Price. Many hotels will increase their prices during the summer, but the price here is actually the same as the last two stays, which is in line with psychological expectations.
2. Environment. With a height above the 36th floor and super-large floor-to-ceiling glass, staying in the hotel is basically equivalent to climbing the tower. The family can enjoy the scenery at any time from check-in to breakfast every day and returning to the room to sleep, extra points! The hotel facilities are well maintained, not too old, clean, natural and comfortable.
3. Facilities. Considering the high temperature and hot weather before traveling, you can swim in the hotel if you don‚Äôt want to go out. The indoor swimming pool on the 48th floor here is 25 meters long.
4. Traffic. Since I drive by myself every time I come, the indoor parking lot is on the 2nd floor, and the ventilation and ventilation will not smell bad, which is a plus for me personally. But this time I also found out that the "Shenzhen University Station" of Metro Line 1 is on the "minus one" floor, and the hotel elevator goes straight down to fry chicken, which is convenient. On the night of check-in, the Window of the World is just three stops away by subway, and you are not afraid of traffic restrictions or typhoons from other places. Shenzhen's most popular Vientiane World is just 2 kilometers away, and it takes only 10 minutes to drive there. The location is very good.
5. Catering. I only ate the buffet for breakfast and lunch, and there was no big surprise, so there is no need to come here for the buffet. There is also a Chinese restaurant in the hotel, but I haven't tried it. There is a yakiniku restaurant on the platform on the 3rd floor, and you can go to the cafeteria late at night, but every time I am hungry, I order takeaway directly, and it is very convenient to pick up the food at the express cabinet downstairs.
6. Service. The hotel front desk, restaurant waiters and room attendants were all very polite and amiable, of course I only judge what I encountered. The aunt in the room gave me a few more bottles of water every day, and changed the towels very diligently. Monica Lynn's service is very good.
7. Surprise. As mentioned before, I will be given two additional breakfasts, but I am not sure that the other party still remembers it when I made the reservation this time. As a result, the hotel sales said that everything promised to the guests would be recorded, and not only did they provide two additional breakfasts, but also upgraded the room type for free, so that I only need to book the cheapest room type, which is very considerate. When I checked in, I found out that I stayed in the hotel for two nights and even served breakfast for two days, which was a pleasant surprise. Of course, if they only delivered breakfast one day, I would also give them full marks for keeping their word. I think a five-star hotel should have the service attitude and tolerance. In addition, I don‚Äôt know if I heard it wrong. When I had breakfast on the third day, I vaguely heard the restaurant manager call my surname "Mr. XX". If it is true, I think this kind of service is worth my next visit.

To sum up, although Crowne Plaza is not a particularly high-end series in the Marriott Group, I will basically not go to several Crowne Plazas in Guangzhou because they are relatively old. But the deep iron hotel gave me a really good feeling, comfortable and safe, and the price is also within a reasonable range.

Service: The service at the front desk of the hotel is fast and comprehensive, especially the receptionist named Terry, who is warm and thoughtful and worthy of praise.
Most of the mid-to-high-end hotels in Shenzhen have stayed once. Personally, I think the Shenzhen Railway is the most cost-effective, and it is worth recommending. PS: The night view of the hotel is very good. You can have a panoramic view of the bustling Nanshan District night view, and the dim lights in the tranquility are the most charming.
